# Jon - Arryn_3
agot_init_canon_child_Arryn_3 = {
	if = {
		limit = { is_alive = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { is_adult = no}
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:pensive AGE = childhood_personality_age }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:just AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_1_year }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:honest AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_2_year }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:diligent AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_3_year }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:null AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_4_year }

			agot_canon_children_schedule_education_effect = { EDUCATION = flag:education_diplomacy_4 }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_prowess_education_effect = { EDUCATION = flag:education_martial_prowess_2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { agot_canon_children_enabled_trigger = yes }
			create_story = { type = story_agot_canon_children_Arryn_3 }
		}
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = { is_adult = no}
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:bossy AGE = childhood_personality_age }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:stubborn AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_1_year }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:diligent AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_2_year }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:patient AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_3_year }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:authoritative AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_4_year }

			agot_canon_children_schedule_education_effect = { EDUCATION = flag:education_martial_3 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { agot_canon_children_enabled_trigger = yes }
			create_story = { type = story_agot_canon_children_Greyjoy_1 }
		}
	}
}

			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:deceitful AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_2_year }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:brave AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_3_year }
			agot_canon_children_schedule_trait_effect = { TRAIT = flag:null AGE = agot_canon_children_trait_4_year }

		}
